// expires in 30 days\n  var expires = \"expires=\" + d.toUTCString();\n\n  if(window.site_region == 'NZ'){\n    document.cookie = \"recent_search=\" + newCookieString + \"; \" + expires + '; domain=.'+ _udn +'; i < dataList.length; i++) {\n    item = dataList[i];\n\n    blockInsert = recentSearchBlock.replace('{{DEPARTURE_NAME}}', item.departure_name);\n    blockInsert = blockInsert.replace('{{DESTINATION_NAME}}', item.destination_name);\n    blockInsert = blockInsert.replace('{{FLIGHT_TYPE}}', item.flight_type == \"ONEWAY\" ? linkURL.replace('{{FLIGHT_TYPE}}', item.flight_type);\n    linkURL = linkURL.replace('{{NUM_ADULT}}', item.numAdults);\n    linkURL = linkURL.replace('{{NUM_CHILDREN}}', item.numChildren);\n    linkURL = linkURL.replace('{{NUM_INFANTS}}', item.numInfants);\n    linkURL = linkURL.replace('{{DATE_OUT}}', item.date_out);\n    linkURL = linkURL.replace('{{DATE_BACK}}', item.date_in);\n\n    blockInsert = blockInsert.replace('{{SEARCH_LINK}}', linkURL);\n\n    resultContainer.append(blockInsert);\n  };\n}\n\nfunction initializeSlider() {\n    // initialize slider once content has been parseInt(dateParts[2]), 0, 0, 0, 0);\n}\n\nfunction formatTripDate(yyyymmdd) {\n  var monthNames = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'];\n  var dayNames = ['Sun','Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat'];\n  var dateParts = yyyymmdd.split('-');\n  var nativeDate = new Date(parseInt(dateParts[0]), parseInt(dateParts[1])-1, parseInt(dateParts[2]));\n\n  return dayNames[nativeDate.getDay()] + \" \" + nativeDate.getDate() + \" \" + monthNames[nativeDate.getMonth()];\n}\n\nfunction formatURLDate(dateIn) {\n  var tmp = dateIn.split('-');\n  return  parseInt(tmp[2]) + '/' + parseInt(tmp[1]) + '/' + parseInt(tmp[0]);\n}\n\nfunction processCookie(rawCookie)\n{\n  var dtNow = new Date();  \n  var rawJSON = decodeURIComponent(rawCookie);\n  var cookieData = JSON.parse(rawJSON);\n  var newData = [];\n  var idx = 0; // index should start from one\n  for (var keys in cookieData) {\n    ++idx;\n    var item = cookieData[keys];\n    var \"number_travellers\": tripDetail.passengerNumber + \" adults\",\n        \"numAdults\": tripDetail.passengerNumber,\n        \"numChildren\": tripDetail.passengerNumberChild,\n        \"numInfants\": tripDetail.passengerNumberInfant,\n        \"travel_dates\": returnTripType ?\n                        formatTripDate(tripDetail.depDate) + \" - \" + formatTripDate(tripDetail.retDate) :\n                        formatTripDate(tripDetail.depDate),\n        \"date_out\" : formatURLDate(tripDetail.depDate),\n        \"date_in\" : returnTripType ? formatURLDate(tripDetail.retDate) : ''\n      };\n      if (parseInt(newEntry.numChildren) + parseInt(newEntry.numInfants) == 0) {\n          newEntry.number_travellers = parseInt(newEntry.numAdults) + \" adults\";\n      } else {\n          newEntry.number_travellers = (parseInt(newEntry.numAdults) + parseInt(newEntry.numChildren) +\n              parseInt(newEntry.numInfants)) + \" travellers\";\n      }\n      var depDate = getDatefromYYYYmmdd(tripDetail.depDate);\n      if (depDate > dtNow) newData.push(newEntry);\n    };\n  };\n\n  return newData;\n}\n\nfunction processCookieNZ(rawCookie)\n{\n  var dtNow = new {\n    ++idx;\n    var item = cookieData[keys];\n    \n    if (\"object\" === typeof(item)) {\n      var returnTripType = (item.tripType.toUpperCase() === \"RETURN\");\n\n      var newEntry = {\n newEntry.number_travellers = (parseInt(newEntry.numAdults) + parseInt(newEntry.numChildren) +\n              parseInt(newEntry.numInfants)) + \" travellers\";\n      }\n\n      var depDate = }\n}\n\nfunction showRecentSearches()\n{\n  var searchesCookie = getCookie(cookieName);\n  if (searchesCookie.length > 9) {\n    wj_recent_search_data = processCookie(searchesCookie);\n  };\n\n  if
